互联网技术/架构/团队

svn web管理之Subversion Edge

2016-11-30 devops svn

Subversion Edge 5.1.4

A certified software stack containing the latest versions of Subversion, Apache, and ViewVC.

Platforms: Red Hat Enterprise Linux 6.x - 7.x, CentOS 6.x - 7.x

注册账户

[http://www.collab.net/downloads/subversion](http://www.collab.net/downloads/subversion)

[http://www.collabnet.cn/downloads/subversion](http://www.collabnet.cn/downloads/subversion)

[https://ctf.open.collab.net/sf/wiki/do/viewPage/projects.svnedge/wiki/Release_5.1.4](https://ctf.open.collab.net/sf/wiki/do/viewPage/projects.svnedge/wiki/Release_5.1.4)

安装JDK

安装Python 2.7(默认有)

安装配置CollabNetSubversionEdge

IMPORTANT: Do not untar CollabNet Subversion Edge using root or sudo.&nbsp; This

&nbsp;&nbsp; will cause the UID/GID on the files to carry the values from our build

&nbsp;&nbsp; system instead of being reset.

<span style="font-size: 20px;">步骤：</span>

useradd&nbsp;&nbsp; svn

passwd svn ---&gt; 123456

mkdir -p /data/svn

chown -R svn:svn /data/svn

chmod -R 770 /data/svn

&nbsp;

把svn群组下的用户加入到sudo组

visudo

找到 root ALL=(ALL) ALL，在下一行加入svn ALL=(ALL) ALL，保存退出。

上传CollabNetSubversionEdge-5.1.4_linux-x86_64.tar.gz 到/tmp目录

用svn用户解压

su svn

tar -zxvf CollabNetSubversionEdge-5.1.4_linux-x86_64.tar.gz -C /data/svn

编辑cscn配置文件

cp /data/svn/csvn/data/conf/csvn.conf.dist /data/svn/csvn/data/conf/csvn.conf

vi /data/svn/csvn/data/conf/csvn.conf

将: #RUN_AS_USER=

改为: RUN_AS_USER=svn

将: #JAVA_HOME=

改为: JAVA_HOME=/usr/java/jdk1.8.0_45

安装csvn

添加环境变量:

vi /etc/profile

在文件最后加入:

PATH=$PATH:/data/svn/csvn/bin

export PATH

&nbsp; ##

source /etc/profile

###

exit (退出svnroot用户,回到root用户)

cd /data/svn/csvn/

sudo -E bin/csvn install

启动csvn

su svn

cd /data/svn/csvn/bin/

csvn start&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; //启动svn

csvn console&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; //如果执行bin/csvn start不能正常启动，尝试该操作

启动svn：也可以在svn控制台启动

csvn-httpd start

启动成功之后，默认管理员登录地址：[http://localhost:3343/csvn](http://localhost:3343/csvn)

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; - 用户名：admin

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; - 密码：admin

Subversion Edge also starts an SSL-protected version using a self-signed SSL

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; certificate.&nbsp; You can access the SSL version on this URL:

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Address: [https://localhost:4434/csvn](https://localhost:4434/csvn)

&nbsp;Optional.

&nbsp;Configure the Apache Subversion server to start automatically when

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; the system boots.

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; $ cd csvn

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; $ sudo bin/csvn-httpd install

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; It is recommend that you login to the Edge console and configure and start the

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Apache server via the web UI before you perform this step.
